add_namespace = usb
add_namespace = bdnspch
add_namespace = nss
country_event = {
	id = usb.1
	title = usb.1.t
	desc = usb.1.desc
	picture = GFX_USB_biden_death
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = USB
	}
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event usb.1 immediate"
			kill_country_leader = yes
			country_event = {
				id = usb.57
				days = 14
			}
			add_ideas = USB_tim_walz_hog
			clr_country_flag = USB_biden_stays_2024
			set_country_flag = USB_resigned_biden_flag
			set_country_flag = USB_biden_died_flag
			add_country_leader_trait = USB_biden_1_off
			add_country_leader_trait = USB_biden_2_off
			add_country_leader_trait = USB_biden_3_off
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = usb.1.a
		effect_tooltip = {
			create_country_leader = {
				name = USB_kamala_harris_char
				picture = "portrait_USA_kamala_harris.dds"
				ideology = neoliberalism
			}
		}
	}
}

#Innovationists Propose A Spending Bill
country_event = {
	id = usb.31
	title = usb.31.t
	desc = usb.31.desc
	picture = GFX_USB_congress_2
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = USB
	}
	#immediate = {
	#	hidden_effect = {
	#	}
	#}
	option = {
		#Pass The Bill
		name = usb.31.a
		set_temp_variable = {
			var = USB_influence_ino_var_temp
			value = -0.1
		}
		USB_add_influence_ino = yes
		set_temp_variable = {
			var = USB_support_ino_var_temp
			value = 0.05
		}
		USB_add_support_ino = yes
		set_temp_variable = {
			var = USB_support_con_var_temp
			value = 0.025
		}
		USB_add_support_con = yes
		set_temp_variable = {
			var = USB_support_neo_var_temp
			value = 0.025
		}
		USB_add_support_neo = yes
		set_temp_variable = {
			var = USB_support_pro_var_temp
			value = -0.05
		}
		USB_add_support_pro = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_idea = USB_ino_spending_bill_idea
				}
			}
			add_timed_idea = {
				idea = USB_ino_spending_bill_idea
				days = 100
			}
			set_temp_variable = {
				var = debt_var_temp
				value = 20
			}
			add_debt = yes
		}
		else = {
			modify_timed_idea = {
				idea = USB_ino_spending_bill_idea
				days = 100
			}
			set_temp_variable = {
				var = debt_var_temp
				value = 10
			}
			add_debt = yes
		}
	}
	option = {
		#Veto The Bill
		name = usb.31.b
		trigger = {
			check_variable = {
				var = USB_influence_ino_var
				value = 0.6
				compare = less_than
			}
		}
		add_political_power = -50
		set_temp_variable = {
			var = USB_influence_ino_var_temp
			value = -0.05
		}
		USB_add_influence_ino = yes
		set_temp_variable = {
			var = USB_support_ino_var_temp
			value = -0.05
		}
		USB_add_support_ino = yes
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = usb.2
	title = usb.2.t
	desc = usb.2.desc
	picture = GFX_USB_congress_4

		tag = USB
	}
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_temp_variable = {
				var = USB_corporate_influence_var_temp
				value = -0.05
			}
			USB_add_corporate_influence = yes
		}
	}
	option = {
		#Pass The Bill
		name = usb.2.a
		set_temp_variable = {
			var = USB_influence_pro_var_temp
			value = -0.1
		}
		USB_add_influence_pro = yes
		set_temp_variable = {
			var = USB_support_pro_var_temp
			value = 0.05
		}

			var = USB_support_neo_var_temp
			value = 0.025
		}
		USB_add_support_neo = yes
		set_temp_variable = {
			var = USB_support_con_var_temp
			value = -0.05
		}
		USB_add_support_con = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = USB_innovationist_enable_flag
			}
			set_temp_variable = {
				var = USB_support_ino_var_temp
				value = -0.025
			}
			USB_add_support_ino = yes
		}

					has_idea = USB_pro_spending_bill_idea
				}

			add_timed_idea = {
				idea = USB_pro_spending_bill_idea
				days = 100
			}
			set_temp_variable = {
				var = debt_var_temp

			}

		else = {
			modify_timed_idea = {
				idea = USB_pro_spending_bill_idea
				days = 100
			}
			set_temp_variable = {
				var = debt_var_temp
				value = 10
			}
			add_debt = yes
		}
	}
	option = {
		#Veto The Bill
		name = usb.2.b
		trigger = {
			check_variable = {
				var = USB_influence_pro_var
				value = 0.6
				compare = less_than
			}
		}
		add_political_power = -50
		set_temp_variable = {
			var = USB_influence_pro_var_temp
			value = -0.05
		}
		USB_add_influence_pro = yes
		set_temp_variable = {
			var = USB_support_pro_var_temp
			value = -0.05
		}
		USB_add_support_pro = yes
	}

	id = usb.11

	desc = usb.11.desc

		tag = USB

			scoped_play_song = "nonstopviolence"

		tag = USB
	}

		hidden_effect = {
		}
	}
	option = {
		#The Coup Fails
		name = usb.12.a
		add_political_power = -100
		add_stability = -0.1
		custom_effect_tooltip = USB_corporate_coup_fails_tooltip
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_stability < 0.2
				}
				country_event = {
					id = usb.16
					days = 10
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		#The Coup Succeeds
		name = usb.12.b
		add_political_power = -50
		add_stability = -0.05
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = usb.17
				days = 2
			}
		}
	}
}

#Biden Resigns
country_event = {
	id = usb.17
	title = usb.17.t
	desc = usb.17.desc
	picture = GFX_USB_white_house_media_room
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = USB
	}
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = USB_corporate_government_flag
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_completed_focus = USB_corporate_constitution
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = authoritarian_democrat
					popularity = 0.3
				}
			}
			else = {
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = authoritarian_democrat
					popularity = 0.4
				}
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = authoritarian_democrat
				elections_allowed = no
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = USB_corporate_government_flag
						has_idea = USB_embraced_the_board_idea
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = USB_corporate_government_flag
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = USB_higher_corporate_influence_idea
					add_idea = USB_corporate_government_idea
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = USB_innovationist_enable_flag
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = USB_innovationist_enable_flag
				add_dynamic_modifier = {
					modifier = USB_ino_influence_dynamic
				}
				set_temp_variable = {
					var = USB_influence_ino_var_temp
					value = 0.4
				}
				USB_add_influence_ino = yes
				set_temp_variable = {
					var = USB_support_ino_var_temp
					value = 0.7
				}
				USB_add_support_ino = yes
			}
			add_ideas = {
				USB_howard_wolfson_hog
				USB_al_gore_for
				USB_lauren_zabierek_int
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = authoritarian_democrat
				long_name = USB_innovationist_party_long
				name = USB_innovationist_party
			}
			set_power_balance_gfx = {
				id = USB_trust_bop
				side = USB_good_side
				gfx = GFX_USB_bop_high_pop_INO
			}
			set_power_balance_gfx = {
				id = USB_trust_bop
				side = USB_bad_side
				gfx = GFX_USB_bop_low_pop_INO
			}
			remove_mission = USB_corporate_influence_mission
			scoped_play_song = "virtualinsanity"
			country_event = {
				id = usb.126
				days = 35
				random_days = 35
			}
			country_event = {
				id = usb.46
				days = 25
				random_days = 25
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		#Yikes
		name = usb.17.a
		effect_tooltip = {
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = authoritarian_democrat
				elections_allowed = no
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = USB_corporate_government_idea
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = USB_higher_corporate_influence_idea
					add_idea = USB_corporate_government_idea
				}
			}
		}
		focus_unlock = yes
		custom_effect_tooltip = USB_unlock_potus_agendas
		add_country_leader_trait = USB_bloomberg_1_off
		add_country_leader_trait = USB_bloomberg_2_off
		add_country_leader_trait = USB_bloomberg_3_off
	}
}

	}

			clr_global_flag = USA_shattered_union_global

			USA_civil_war_over = yes

				target = USN
				transfer_troops = yes
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = USN
				}
				add_core_of = USB
				remove_core_of = USN
			}

			#	id = usb.46
			#	days = 45
			#	random_days = 35
			#}
			delete_unit_template_and_units = {
				division_template = "Volunteer Militia"
			}
			delete_unit_template_and_units = {
				division_template = "Motorized Militia"
			}

				news_event = {
					id = news.575
					hours = 6
				}
				set_portraits = {

		tag = USB
	}
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event bdnspch.17 immediate"
			USB_speech_quality_effect = yes
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = bdnspch.17.a
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = USB_good_memory_speech_flag
		}
		add_days_mission_timeout = {
			mission = USB_biden_health_timer_mission
			days = 7
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = USB_good_speech_texticon_3_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			USB_clear_speech_effect = yes
		}
		add_political_power = 25
		set_temp_variable = {
			var = income_var_temp
			value = 0.25
		}

		set_temp_variable = {
			var = USB_support_con_var_temp
			value = 0.02
		}
		USB_add_support_con = yes
	}

			mission = USB_biden_health_timer_mission
			days = -14
		}

			value = -0.02
		}

		hidden_effect = {
			USB_clear_speech_effect = yes
		}
	}
	option = {

			always = no

			base = 100
			modifier = {
			    factor = 0
			    has_game_rule = {
			        rule = The_Biden_Resign
			        option = The_Biden_Resign_NO
			    }
			}

	id = bdnspch.27
	title = bdnspch.27.t
	desc = bdnspch.27.d
	picture = GFX_USB_speech_3
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = USB
	}
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event bdnspch.27 immediate"
			USB_speech_quality_effect = yes
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = bdnspch.27.a
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = USB_good_memory_speech_flag
		}
		add_days_mission_timeout = {
			mission = USB_biden_health_timer_mission
			days = 7
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = USB_good_speech_texticon_1_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			USB_clear_speech_effect = yes
		}
		add_political_power = 25
	}
	option = {
		name = bdnspch.27.b
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = USB_bad_memory_speech_flag
		}
		add_days_mission_timeout = {
			mission = USB_biden_health_timer_mission
			days = -14
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = USB_bad_speech_texticon_1_tt
		add_political_power = -10
		hidden_effect = {
			USB_clear_speech_effect = yes
		}
	}
	option = {
		#maybe it's time to retire
		name = bdnspch.1.c
		custom_effect_tooltip = USB_bad_speech_texticon_1_tt
		trigger = {
			always = no
			has_country_flag = USB_bad_memory_speech_flag
			has_country_leader_with_trait = hos_blank
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
			modifier = {
			    factor = 0
			    has_game_rule = {
			        rule = The_Biden_Resign
			        option = The_Biden_Resign_NO
			    }
			}
		}
		country_event = {
			id = usb.58
			days = 14
		}
		#Biden Resigns
		custom_effect_tooltip = USB_bad_speech_texticon_2_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			USB_clear_speech_effect = yes
		}
	}
}

	id = nss.21
	title = nss.21.t
	desc = nss.21.d
	picture = GFX_USB_nordhaus
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = USB
	}
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = USB_loose_ends_nordhaus_dead_flag
			add_to_variable = {
				var = USB_loose_ends_public_awareness_var
				value = -0.05
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = nss.21.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = USB_judas_gambit_flag
			}
			set_temp_variable = {
				var = USB_judas_speed_var_temp
				value = 5
			}
			USB_add_judas_speed = yes
		}
		set_temp_variable = {
			var = USB_NSS_public_awareness_var_temp
			value = -0.05
		}
		USB_add_public_awareness = yes
		custom_effect_tooltip = USB_weaken_reshuffle_tt
	}
}

#Silent Coup in Canada
country_event = {
	id = nss.33
	title = nss.33.t
	desc = nss.33.d
	picture = GFX_USB_canada_coup
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = USB
	}
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			CAN = {
				get_current_government_type = yes
				USB = {
					puppet = PREV
				}
				restore_previous_government_type = yes
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = nationalist
					elections_allowed = yes
				}
				add_country_leader_role = {
					character = CAN_justin_trudeau
					promote_leader = yes
					country_leader = {
						ideology = pax_americana_ultraglobalism
					}
				}
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = nationalist
					long_name = CAN_cognoscenti_long
					name = CAN_social_liberal_party
				}
				set_portraits = {
					character = CAN_justin_trudeau
					civilian = {
						large = "gfx/leaders/CAN/CAN_justin_trudeau_beard.png"
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = nss.33.a
	}
}

#War with Russia
country_event = {
	id = nss.34
	title = nss.34.t
	desc = nss.34.d
	picture = GFX_USB_icy_wastes
	fire_only_once = yes
	#is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = USB
		USB = { has_war_with = SOV }
	}
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = USB_SOV_war_flag
			if = {
				limit = {
					SOV = {
						is_ai = yes
					}
				}
				SOV = {
					add_ideas = SOV_medvedev_can_win
					load_oob = "SOV_ai_help"
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = nss.34.a
		focus_unlock = yes
	}
}

#Third Gulf War
country_event = {
	id = nss.37
	title = nss.37.t
	desc = nss.37.d
	picture = GFX_USB_mena
	fire_only_once = yes
	#is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = USB
		USB = {
			OR = {
				has_war_with = PER
				has_war_with = IRQ
				has_war_with = BUK
				has_war_with = ABK
				has_war_with = FIA
				has_war_with = SYR
				has_war_with = JAH
				has_war_with = TAL
				has_war_with = MUS
			}
		}
	}
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = USB_ME_war_flag
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					exists = yes
					OR = {
						tag = PER
						tag = HOU
						tag = IRQ
						tag = BUK
						tag = ABK
						tag = FIA
						tag = SYR
						tag = JAH
					}
				}
				add_ideas = USB_against_the_invader_idea
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					exists = yes
					OR = {
						tag = IRQ
						tag = BUK
						tag = ABK
						tag = FIA
					}
				}
				load_oob = "IRQ_2020"
			}
			PER = {
				load_oob = "PER_2020"
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_completed_custom_achievement = {
						mod = the_fire_rises
						achievement = renovatio_imperii
					}
				}
				country_event = {
					id = nss.97
					days = 15
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = nss.37.a
		focus_unlock = yes
	}
}

#Demand to leave the BRI
country_event = {
	id = nss.38
	title = nss.38.t
	desc = nss.38.d
	picture = GFX_USB_pravda
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = USB
	}
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = nss.38.a
		USB = {
			add_political_power = 20
		}
		clr_country_flag = PRC_BRI_member_flag
		remove_ideas = {
			PRC_BRI_member
		}
		PRC = {
			add_to_variable = {
				PRC_BRI_number_of_members = -1
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				PRC_BRI_consumer_goods_factor = 0.001
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				PRC_BRI_income_growth_factor = -0.001
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				PRC_BRI_lend_lease_tension = 0.01
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				PRC_BRI_poverty_development_monthly = -0.001
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				PRC_BRI_industrial_development_monthly = -0.001
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				PRC_BRI_global_building_slots_factor = -0.005
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				PRC_BRI_production_speed_buildings_factor = -0.005
			}
		}
		remove_from_array = {
			PRC.PRC_BRI_members = THIS
		}
		remove_opinion_modifier = {
			target = PRC
			modifier = friendship_of_peoples
		}
		PRC = {
			remove_opinion_modifier = {
				target = ROOT
				modifier = friendship_of_peoples
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = nss.38.b
		add_political_power = 20
	}
}

#NSS Elections
country_event = {
	id = nss.41
	title = nss.41.t
	desc = nss.41.d
	picture = GFX_USB_election_nss
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = USB
		has_country_flag = USB_NSS_flag
		date < 2033.01.01
	}
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			clr_country_flag = USB_NSS_newsom_flag
			clr_country_flag = USB_NSS_harris_flag
			clr_country_flag = USB_NSS_austin_flag
			clr_country_flag = USB_NSS_bolton_flag
			clr_country_flag = USB_NSS_milley_flag
			clr_country_flag = USB_NSS_blinken_flag
			clr_country_flag = USB_NSS_hunter_flag
			clr_country_flag = USB_NSS_pelosi_flag
			clr_country_flag = USB_NSS_schumer_flag
			clr_country_flag = USB_NSS_cheney_flag
			if = {
				limit = {
					date > 2025.01.01
				}
				country_event = {
					id = nss.42
					days = 78
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #Incumbent Victory
		name = nss.41.a
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				date < 2025.01.01
				AND = {
					date > 2029.01.01
					date < 2033.01.01
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #Gavin Newsom
		name = nss.41.b
		trigger = {
			date > 2025.01.01
			date < 2029.01.01
			check_variable = {
				var = USB_the_blood_influence_var
				value = 0.4
				compare = less_than
			}
			check_variable = {
				var = USB_the_body_influence_var
				value = 0.4
				compare = less_than
			}
			check_variable = {
				var = USB_the_mind_influence_var
				value = 0.4
				compare = less_than
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = USB_NSS_newsom_flag
	}
	option = { #Mitt Romney
		name = nss.41.c
		trigger = {
			date > 2025.01.01
			date < 2029.01.01
			check_variable = {
				var = USB_the_blood_influence_var
				value = 0.4
				compare = less_than
			}
			check_variable = {
				var = USB_the_body_influence_var
				value = 0.4
				compare = less_than
			}
			check_variable = {
				var = USB_the_mind_influence_var
				value = 0.5
				compare = less_than
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = USB_NSS_romney_flag
	}
	option = { #Lloyd Austin
		name = nss.41.e
		trigger = {
			date > 2025.01.01
			date < 2029.01.01
			check_variable = {
				var = USB_the_mind_influence_var
				value = 0.4
				compare = greater_than_or_equals
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = USB_NSS_austin_flag
	}
	option = { #John Bolton
		name = nss.41.f
		trigger = {
			date > 2025.01.01
			date < 2029.01.01
			check_variable = {
				var = USB_the_body_influence_var
				value = 0.4
				compare = greater_than_or_equals
			}
		}

	desc = nss.65.d

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

		tag = USB
	}

		hidden_effect = {
			BRA = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_government = conservative 
					}
					set_country_flag = USB_bolsonaro_coup_flag
				}
				else = {
					set_country_flag = USB_lula_coup_flag
				}
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = nationalist
					elections_allowed = no
				}
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = nationalist
					name = BRA_military_party
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = nationalist
					popularity = 0.45
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = USB_bolsonaro_coup_flag
					}
					create_country_leader = {
						name = BRA_edson_l_pujol_char
						picture = "gfx/leaders/BRA/BRA_edson_l_pujol.png"
						ideology = military_junta
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = USB_lula_coup_flag
					}
					create_country_leader = {
						name = BRA_tomas_r_paiva_char
						picture = "gfx/leaders/BRA/BRA_tomas_r_paiva.png"
						ideology = military_junta
					}
				}
			}
			country_event = {
				id = nss.96
				days = 35
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = nss.65.a
	}

#Burns in Hell
country_event = {
	id = nss.102
	title = nss.102.t
	desc = nss.102.d
	picture = GFX_USB_world_is_yours
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = USB
	}
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			load_focus_tree = generic_focus
			clr_country_flag = USB_loose_ends_flag
			remove_mission = USB_deck_reshuffle_mission
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_war_with = USB
				}
				white_peace = USB
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					is_puppet_of = USB
				}
				USB = {
					end_puppet = PREV
				}
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						USA_is_washington_state = yes
						USA_is_oregon_state = yes
						USA_is_idaho_state = yes
					}
				}
				transfer_state_to = CAC
				add_core_of = CAC
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						USA_is_california_state = yes
					}
				}
				transfer_state_to = CAL
				add_core_of = CAL
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						USA_is_texas_state = yes
					}
				}
				transfer_state_to = TEX
				add_core_of = TEX
			}
			country_event = {
				id = nss.115
				days = 15
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					GER = {
						has_completed_focus = GER_democracy_falters
					}
				}
				country_event = {
					id = nss.113
					days = 7
				}
			}
			else = {
				country_event = {
					id = nss.114
					days = 7
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = nss.102.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = USB_burns_dies_tt
	}
}

#Government Collapse
country_event = {
	id = nss.115
	title = nss.115.t
	desc = nss.115.d
	picture = GFX_USB_flag_lowered
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = USB
	}
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			USB_kill_em_all = yes
			add_ideas = {
				vacant_hog
				vacant_for
				vacant_eco
				vacant_sec
				vacant_int
				vacant_theorist
			}
			change_economy_type_capitalism = yes
			change_government_type_provisional_government = yes
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = authoritarian_democrat
				elections_allowed = no
			}
			set_popularities = {
				market_liberal = 5
				authoritarian_democrat = 35
				social_liberal = 33
				conservative = 10
				social_democrat = 17
			}
			end_coalition = yes
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = nationalist
				long_name = USB_communist_banned
				name = USB_communist_banned
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = social_democrat
				long_name = USB_social_democrat_party_long
				name = USB_NSS_party
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = social_liberal
				long_name = USB_social_liberal_party_long
				name = USB_NSS_party
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = market_liberal
				long_name = USB_market_liberal_party_long
				name = USB_market_liberal_party
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = conservative
				long_name = USB_conservative_party_long
				name = USB_conservative_party
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = authoritarian_democrat
				long_name = USB_transitional_authority_char
				name = USB_transitional_authority_char
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = USB_transitional_authority_char
				picture = "gfx/leaders/USB/USB_transitional_authority.png"
				ideology = hybrid_regime
			}
			country_event = {
				id = nss.93
				days = 6
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = nss.115.a
	}
}
